3.3.2 Ledetekster eller instruksjoner (1 avvik)
Testregel 3.3.2 (3.3.2 - Nivå A)
CRITICAL

Form input has no label

<input aria-hidden="true" autocomplete="nope" class="sr-only" id="name" name="name" tabindex="-1" type="text"/>
Add a <label> element with for attribute pointing to input id
2.1.1 Tastatur (1 avvik)
Testregel 2.1.1 (2.1.1 - Nivå A)
SERIOUS

Interactive input has tabindex='-1' - not keyboard accessible

<input aria-hidden="true" autocomplete="nope" class="sr-only" id="name" name="name" tabindex="-1" type="text"/>
Remove tabindex='-1' unless element is in an inactive state
1.3.1 Informasjon og relasjoner (2 avvik)
Testregel 1.3.1 (1.3.1 - Nivå A)
MODERATE

Page has 2 main landmarks (should have 1)

<main>
Use only one <main> element per page
Testregel 1.3.1 (1.3.1 - Nivå A)
MODERATE

List contains non-li elements: ['template']

<ul class="wrapper"> <template :key="item.id" x-for="item in playlist"> <li> <button @click="select(item.id)" x-bind:class="isCurrentTrack(item.id) ? 'font-bold' : ''" x-text="item.title"></button> <b
List elements (ul, ol) should only contain li children
1.4.2 Styring av lyd (4 avvik)
Testregel 1.4.2 (1.4.2 - Nivå A)
CRITICAL

Audio autoplays - may interfere with screen readers

<audio autoplay="" data-player-audio="" preload="metadata"></audio>
Remove autoplay or ensure audio stops within 3 seconds
Testregel 1.4.2 (1.4.2 - Nivå A)
SERIOUS

Audio has no native controls

<audio autoplay="" data-player-audio="" preload="metadata"></audio>
Add controls attribute or provide custom accessible controls
Testregel 1.4.2 (1.4.2 - Nivå A)
CRITICAL

Audio autoplays - may interfere with screen readers

<audio autoplay="" preload="metadata" x-bind:src="currentTrack.url" x-ref="audio"></audio>
Remove autoplay or ensure audio stops within 3 seconds
Testregel 1.4.2 (1.4.2 - Nivå A)
SERIOUS

Audio has no native controls

<audio autoplay="" preload="metadata" x-bind:src="currentTrack.url" x-ref="audio"></audio>
Add controls attribute or provide custom accessible controls
